This JSON object represents a questionnaire with two questions about training effectiveness. The first question asks about the overall effectiveness of the training, and the second question asks about the relevance and up-to-date-ness of the training content and methods. The answer options for both questions are presented as an array of objects, with each object containing an "ANSWER" string property. The "DISPLAY_ORDER" property is used to order the questions.

The questions ask whether the individual feels they have a clear understanding of their career path, whether their current role is a stepping stone, whether they have the skills and qualifications to reach their desired position, whether the company provides necessary support and resources, whether they know about career progression opportunities, whether the company provides clear guidelines, whether they have the opportunity to provide feedback, whether the company understands their career goals, and whether the company understands the skills and qualifications needed to reach those goals.

**On a scale of 1 to 5, how would you rate the health and safety measures currently in place within the company? (1 being very poor, 5 being excellent)**
  - 1
  - 2
  - 3
  - 4
  - 5

  - Yes
  - No
  - Sometimes

  - Yes
  - No

  - No

  - No

The third question is about the accessibility of internal mobility opportunities, and the fourth question asks whether internal mobility opportunities could be improved by providing more training and support. The fifth question is about whether internal mobility opportunities could be improved, and the sixth question asks whether internal mobility opportunities could be improved by providing more training and support. Each question has a unique code, content, type, display order, and a list of possible answers. The type of questions is 1, 2, or 3, which means that the person can choose one answer from a list, choose one or more answers from a list, or rate something. The display order indicates the order in which the questions should be displayed. The possible answers to each question are "Yes, definitely", "Yes, somewhat", "No, not really", and "No, not at all".

This JSON object represents an onboarding experience questionnaire with six questions. The first question is a yes/no question about whether the respondent has been through an onboarding process in this company. The second question is a rating question about the overall onboarding experience. The third question is a yes/no/somewhat question about whether the respondent was provided with a clear onboarding plan. The fourth question is a yes/no/somewhat question about whether the onboarding process helped the respondent understand the company's values, mission, and culture. The fifth question is a yes/no/maybe question about whether the onboarding process could be improved. The sixth question is a reorder question about the specific areas that could be improved in the onboarding process. Each question has a unique code, name, type, and display order, and the answers are stored in a separate array.

These images can be used to create a quiz about work-life balance. The quiz should ask about the following topics:

1. How many hours per day someone works
2. If technology is helping or hurting their work-life balance
3. If they are able to disconnect from work when not at the office
4. What steps they and their company can take to improve work-life balance
5. If the company's policies and culture help them maintain a good work-life balance

Each question should have an image and a corresponding text. The images and text can be used together to create a quiz.

Here is a suggested quiz format:

Q1: How many hours per day do you work?

- 8 hours
- 9 hours
- 10 hours
- More than 10 hours

Q2: Do you feel that technology is helping or hurting your work-life balance?
- Helping
- Neutral
- Hurting

Q3: Are you able to disconnect from work when you are not physically at the office?
- Yes, always
- Yes, sometimes
- No, not often
- No, never

Q4: What steps can you and the company take to improve your work-life balance?

- Allow flexible work schedules
- Limit overtime work
- Implement wellness programs and activities
- Create a culture that supports work-life balance
- Other (please specify)

Q5: Do you feel that the company's policies and culture help you maintain a good work-life balance?
- Yes
- Sometimes
- No

This JSON represents an employee engagement questionnaire with 4 questions. Each question is a choice between 4 possible answers, represented by the `_TF_ANSWERS` array. The `ANSWER` property of each object in this array is a string representing the content of the answer. The `TYPE_ID` property of each question is 1, indicating that this is a question where the respondent can choose one answer from a list. The `DISPLAY_ORDER` property is used to order the questions.
